State O O
of O O
OpenSC O O
I O O
believe O O
that O O
security O O
software O O
should O O
be O O
simple O O
, O O
well O O
designed O O
, O O
well O O

actively O O
maintained O O
by O O

. O O

is O O
usually O O

for O O

( O O

CVE-2009-0368 O O
OpenSC O O
stores O O
private O O
data O O
without O O
proper O O
access O O
restrictions O O
. O O

This O O
could O O
always O O
be O O
turned O O
off O O
with O O
the O O
soft_keygen_allowed O O
in O O

config O O
file O O
. O O

We O O
have O O
not O O
heard O O
of O O
any O O
user O O
of O O
such O O

cards O O
without O O
the O O

to O O

for O O

. O O

OpenSC O O
used O O
to O O

access O O
to O O
a O O

when O O

used O O

at O O
all O O

and O O
not O O

single O O

in O O

. O O
